[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During an automated fuzzing session with Jazzer and libFuzzer, the harness [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExpanderFuzzer` invoked the example decompression logic in [0m                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The problem is a memory exhaustion condition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial-of-service style[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, reported [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`. The fuzzer suggests reproducing with a larger heap [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`-Xmx1710m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that input complexity leads to unbounded resource usage.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The OOM occurs in `LZWInputStream.initializeTables`, called by [0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The OOM stems from LZWInputStream.initializeTables being invoked with [0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m210[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m218[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, allowing an attacker-supplied “maxCodeSize” header to drive table [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocations unbounded, ultimately exhausting the Java heap.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Legitimate “.Z” streams use code sizes in the [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m range and require roughly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m<<[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m…[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m KiB…[0m[1;36m384[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, well under a safe default.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We must continue to support standard-compliant .Z files without performance [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We must avoid breaking downstream code relying on the existing constructors.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno harness or test changes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z.ZCompressorInputStream:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Introduce two new private constants:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m  [0m[1;39m([0m[39mper RFC [0m[1;36m1052[0m[39m .Z spec[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        – DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KiB = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >> [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcomputes to [0m[1;36m384[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Replace the no-arg memory-limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the default constructor:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          public [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream in[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mthis[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Immediately after reading “thirdByte” and computing “maxCodeSize”, add [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unsupported LZW code size: "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Retain the subsequent call to [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Because memoryLimitInKiB is now ≥ [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, the check in LZWInputStream[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m210[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m218[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will enforce an upper bound on table size.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Benefits  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By providing a sane default memory limit [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m384[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we ensure initializeTables[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malways performs its guard check, eliminating unbounded allocations under malicious [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The MAX_SUPPORTED_CODE_SIZE check defends against invalid headers that claim [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplausible bit widths.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Standard .Z archives [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcode sizes [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m consume ≤ DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to decompress successfully.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No downstream or harness code changes are required; the fuzzer entry point [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill calls the same constructors, but now cannot bypass the safety check.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – In the unlikely event of a legitimate .Z file that encodes a custom “[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode beyond [0m[1;36m384[0m[39m KiB requirement, it will still pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrequires ~[0m[1;36m384[0m[39m KiB exactly[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. If[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture specs allow larger codes, adjust DEFAULT_MEMORY_LIMIT accordingly.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Clients that explicitly use the two-arg constructor with –[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to bypass limits [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now continue to do so, preserving backward compatibility for advanced use [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Unit tests should be added to verify both valid streams [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m succeed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand oversized headers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fail with an IOException, as well as that memory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion is caught as a MemoryLimitException.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – LZWInputStream.initializeTables: memory check only triggers when [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB > –[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – ZCompressorInputStream default invokes [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, –[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – RFC [0m[1;36m1052[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.Z format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m limits code sizes to a maximum of [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Similar defense in [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mother compressor implementations[0m[1;39m][0m[39m that employ configurable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource limits.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
